posted:Posted May 5, 2024
msg:Facilities: It has everything it should have, but it's a pity that there are no recreational facilities. In fact, it's okay even if it's charged. Ping-pong and the like can be a bit entertaining.

Environment: It's in the financial district of Wuxi. There are few people and few cars during holidays. I like it very much. Although it's a bit far from the scenic spots, it's not a problem if you drive yourself. The lobby is quite fragrant. But our two executive rooms on different floors have a sour smell on the floor, which is so bad.

Hygiene: The sanitation is pretty good, and the public toilets in the gym are also quite clean.

Service: First of all, I would like to praise the receptionist Summer Banxia who received me. The service is very thoughtful and responsive; in addition, there is Manager Zhang in the Western restaurant. Because I stayed for two days and had a buffet dinner, I had more contact with him and was able to solve problems in time. The other waiters didn't seem to do the warm greetings I wrote in the questionnaire after scanning the questionnaire in the executive lounge. They were all very careless. Even the manager on duty during the two days I was there also confronted me. As a high-end brand of IHG that I trust very much, I am still a little disappointed.
